  * grade_story_102.txt (grade=5.5)
    While the story incorporates all required elements, it struggles with balance—overly elaborate prose sometimes obscures rather than illuminates the narrative. The premise has potential, but execution is hindered by excessive description and telling rather than showing. The world-building shows creative potential, but character development remains shallow, preventing deeper reader engagement.
